The work of a wenbumber is fixing and treating problems with teeth. Iniguez is an orgemier. Gunnels is a wenbumber. The work of an oterer is troubleshooting and identifying problems with vehicles including cars and trucks professionally. Humble is an oterer. Araiza is a ceeper.

The work of a dymer is checking and correcting any problems with eyes and eye sight. Mckellar is a motaswer. The work of a turper is unpacking merchandise when it arrives at the warehouse. Vannoy is a turper. Ficklin is a pinwer. The work of a pinwer is working in fashion and modeling clothes and accessories. Swoboda is a dymer. The work of a motaswer is preparing food for others in a restaurant.
